local v_u_1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GameState")
local v2 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("GameObjectGui")
local v_u_3 = game:GetService("Players")
local v_u_4 = v_u_3.LocalPlayer
local v_u_5 = game:GetService("StarterGui")
local v6 = v2:WaitForChild("StatusScreen")
local v_u_7 = {}
for _, v8 in ipairs(v6:GetChildren()) do
	v_u_7[v8.Name] = v8
end
local function v_u_12(p9, p10) -- name: SetCharacterTransparency
	if p9 then
		for _, v11 in ipairs(p9:GetDescendants()) do
			if v11:IsA("BillboardGui") then
				v11.Enabled = p10 == 0
			end
			if v11:IsA("BasePart") or v11:IsA("Decal") then
				if v11.Name == "HitBox" then
					if p10 == 1 then
						v11.Transparency = 1
					else
						v11.Transparency = game.ReplicatedStorage.HitBox.Transparency
					end
				elseif v11.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
					v11.Transparency = p10
				end
			end
		end
	end
end
local function v_u_16(p13) -- name: HideOthers
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_12
	local v14 = p13 and 1 or 0
	for _, v15 in ipairs(v_u_3:GetPlayers()) do
		if v15 ~= v_u_4 and v15.Character then
			v_u_12(v15.Character, v14)
		end
	end
end
local function v19() -- name: UpdateUI
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_5
	local v17 = v_u_1:GetAttribute("Status")
	local v18 = v_u_1:GetAttribute("TimeLeft")
	v_u_7.Status.Text = v17
	v_u_7.Time.Text = v18
	if v17 == "Blue Team Wins!" then
		v_u_7.Blue.Visible = true
		v_u_7.Status.Visible = false
		v_u_7.Time.Visible = false
		return
	elseif v17 == "Red Team Wins!" then
		v_u_7.Red.Visible = true
		v_u_7.Status.Visible = false
		v_u_7.Time.Visible = false
		return
	elseif v17 == "Draw!" then
		v_u_7.Draw.Visible = true
		v_u_7.Status.Visible = false
		v_u_7.Time.Visible = false
		return
	else
		v_u_7.Draw.Visible = false
		v_u_7.Blue.Visible = false
		v_u_7.Red.Visible = false
		if v17 == "Intermission" and tonumber(v18) < 1 then
			v_u_7.Status.Visible = false
			v_u_7.Time.Visible = false
		else
			v_u_7.Status.Visible = true
			v_u_7.Time.Visible = true
		end
		if v17 == "Choosing" then
			v_u_16(true)
			v_u_5:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Chat, false)
			v_u_5:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.PlayerList, false)
		else
			v_u_16(false)
			v_u_5:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Chat, true)
			v_u_5:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.PlayerList, true)
		end
	end
end
v_u_1:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Status"):Connect(v19)
v_u_1:GetAttributeChangedSignal("TimeLeft"):Connect(v19)
v2.Enabled = true
v2.StatusScreen.Visible = true
for _, v20 in v_u_7 do
	v20.Visible = false
end
v19()

local v_u_2 = game:GetService("Players")
local v_u_3 = { 110978061, 1037059083 }
function v1.OnIncomingMessage(p4)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3
	local v5 = Instance.new("TextChatMessageProperties")
	local v6 = p4.TextSource and v_u_2:GetPlayerByUserId(p4.TextSource.UserId)
	if v6 then
		local v7 = v6:GetAttribute("IsVip")
		local v8 = table.find(v_u_3, v6.UserId)
		if v8 then
			v5.PrefixText = "<font face=\'FredokaOne\' color=\'#FF0000\'>[Owner]</font> " .. p4.PrefixText
		elseif v7 then
			v5.PrefixText = "<font face=\'FredokaOne\' color=\'#FFD700\'>[VIP]</font> " .. p4.PrefixText
		end
		if v8 then
			v5.Text = "<font color=\'#00FFFF\'>" .. p4.Text .. "</font>"
			return v5
		end
		if v7 then
			v5.Text = "<font color=\'#FFD700\'>" .. p4.Text .. "</font>"
		end
	end
	return v5
end

	end

	["Blue"] = -230,

function v_u_1.GetRewardItem() -- name: GetRewardItem

end
function v_u_1.Setup() -- name: Setup
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
	local v12 = v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("SETUP")
	for _, v13 in pairs(v12) do

function v_u_1.Spin() -- name: Spin
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6
	if v_u_9 then
		v_u_10.Visible = false
		v_u_9 = false
		local v17 = v_u_3.Rotation
		local v18 = v_u_1.GetRewardItem()
		if not v18 then
			v_u_10.Visible = true
			v_u_9 = true
			v_u_1.ShowError()
			return nil
		end
		local v19 = v17 + (v_u_11[v18[3]] - v17) % 360 + 7200
		local v20 = game:GetService("TweenService")
		local v21 = TweenInfo.new(9, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
		game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Play()
		local v22 = v20:Create(v_u_3, v21, {
			["Rotation"] = v19
		})
		v22:Play()
		v22.Completed:Wait()
		if v18[4] == "WEAPONS" then
			game.SoundService["Mythical Summon"]:Play()
			local v23 = "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'>[Server Announcement]: " .. game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. " Spinned A </font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FF0000" .. "\'>" .. "Mythical" .. "</font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'> Weapon " .. v18[1] .. "</font>"
			if game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Announce") then
				game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Announce:FireServer(v23)
			end
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_8, v18[1], v18[2])
		else
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_7, v18[1], v18[2])
		end
		v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("REWARD")
		v_u_9 = true
		v_u_10.Visible = true
	end
end
function v_u_1.ShowError() -- name: ShowError
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2
	local v_u_24 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("SpinError")
	local v_u_25 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Error")
	v_u_24.Visible = false
	(function() -- name: showWarning
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_25
		local v_u_26 = v_u_24:Clone()
		v_u_26.Parent = v_u_24.Parent
		v_u_26.Visible = true
		v_u_26.TextTransparency = 1
		v_u_26.Size = UDim2.fromScale(0.147, 0.065)
		v_u_26.Position = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
		v_u_25:Play()
		game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v_u_26, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
			["TextTransparency"] = 0,
			["Size"] = nil,
			["Position"] = nil,
			["Size"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.22, 0.065),
			["Position"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
		}):Play()
		task.delay(2.5, function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_26
			if v_u_26 then
				v_u_26:Destroy()
			end
		end)
	end)()
end

	p27.Image.Image = p29
	p27.RewardText.Text = p28
	p27.Visible = false
	local v30 = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local v31 = {
		["Size"] = p27.Size
	}
	p27.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	task.wait(0.1)
	p27.Visible = true
	v30:Create(p27, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), v31):Play()
	game.SoundService["VIP Weapon Reward"]:Play()
	task.wait(2)
	p27.Visible = false
end
function v_u_1.Start(p32) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6

	v_u_8 = p32.Parent:FindFirstChild("SpecialSpinReward")

		v_u_1.Spin()
	end)
	local v_u_35 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("Claim Free Spin")
	local function v_u_50() -- name: Timer
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_35, (copy) v_u_33
		if v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") == 0 then
			v_u_35.TextLabel.Text = "Claim Free Spin"
			v_u_33.Text = "Claim Free Spin"
		else
			local v36 = v_u_35.TextLabel
			local v37 = v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") or 0
			local v38 = v37 / 3600
			local v39 = math.floor(v38)
			local v40 = v37 % 3600 / 60
			local v41 = math.floor(v40)
			local v42 = v37 % 60
			v36.Text = string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d", v39, v41, v42) .. " For Free Spin"
			local v43 = v_u_33
			local v44 = v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") or 0
			local v45 = v44 / 3600
			local v46 = math.floor(v45)
			local v47 = v44 % 3600 / 60
			local v48 = math.floor(v47)
			local v49 = v44 % 60
			v43.Text = string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d", v46, v48, v49) .. " For Free Spin"
		end
	end
	v_u_50()
	v_u_34:GetAttributeChangedSignal("LastSpinReward"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_50

	end)
	v_u_35.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()

	v_u_34:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Spins"):Connect(function()

	end
end

local function v_u_12(p10, p11) -- name: Unlock
	if p11 and p11 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p11 == "TITLES" then
			if p10:FindFirstChild("LockedButton") then
				p10.LockedButton.Visible = false
			end
			if p10:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
				p10.EquipButton.Visible = true
			end
		end
		return
	elseif p10 then
		p10.WeaponImage.Transparency = 0
		p10.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
		if p10.WeaponImage:FindFirstChild("Locked") then
			p10.WeaponImage.Locked.Visible = false
		end
		p10.EquipButton.Visible = true
		p10.LockedButton.Visible = false
	else
		print("Weapon Frame not Found")
	end
end
local function v_u_18(p13, _, p14) -- name: PrepareInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_6
	if p13 then
		if p14 and p14 == "TITLES" then
			print("nothing")
		else
			local v15 = v_u_7.Samples
			for _, v_u_16 in pairs(p13.Weapons) do
				local v17 = v_u_2.WeaponTemplate.TemplateLocked:Clone()
				v17.Name = v_u_16.weaponName
				v17.WeaponImage.Image.Image = v_u_16.image
				v17.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
				v17.WeaponName.Text = v_u_16.weaponName
				v17.WeaponName.TextColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.Rarity.Text = v_u_16.rarity
				v17.Rarity.TextColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.WeaponImage.Stroke.BackgroundColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.Parent = v_u_2
				v17.Visible = true
				v17.UIGradient.Color = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Gradient
				v17.EquipButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_16
					game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
					v_u_6.EquipWeapon:FireServer(v_u_16.weaponName)
				end)
			end
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
local function v_u_22() -- name: EquipWeapon
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_2
	local v19 = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Equipped")
	if v19 then
		print("Last Weapon was " .. v19)
		if v_u_8 then
			v_u_8.TextLabel.Text = "Equip"
		end
		local v20 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild(v19)
		if v20 then
			print("Weapon Frame found for " .. v19)
			v20.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
			v_u_8 = v20.EquipButton
			print("Equipped Last Equipped")
		else
			print("Weapon Frame not found for " .. v19)
		end
	else
		print("No weapon equipped")
		local v21 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild("Baseball Bat")
		if v21 then
			print("Baseball Frame found")
			v21.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
			v_u_8 = v21.EquipButton
			return true
		end
		print("Baseball Frame not found")
		return
	end
end
function v_u_9.AddToInventory(p23, _, p24) -- name: AddToInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_12, (ref) v_u_5
	if p24 and p24 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p24 == "TITLES" then
			print("TRYING TO FIND FRAME FOR " .. p23)
			local v25 = v_u_5:WaitForChild(p23, (1 / 0))
			if v25 then
				v_u_12(v25, p24)
			end
			print("FOUND AND UNLOCK " .. p23)
		end
		return
	end
	local v26 = nil
	local v27 = 0
	while not v26 do
		v27 = v27 + 1
		if v27 > 3 then
			break
		end
		v26 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild(p23)
		task.wait(1)
	end
	if v26 then
		print("Found Weapon Frame for " .. p23)
		v_u_12(v26, p24)
	else
		warn("Could not find frame for weapon:", p23)
	end
end
function v_u_9.Start(p28, p29) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_22
	v_u_1 = p28
	v_u_2 = v_u_1.Weapon.OutnerFrame.Weapons.InnerFrameLayout
	v_u_3 = p29
	v_u_4 = v_u_3.Titles
	v_u_5 = v_u_4.TitlesFrame
	v_u_6 = game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes
	v_u_7 = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponDatabase)
	v_u_8 = nil
	if v_u_1 then
		require(game.ReplicatedStorage.MainGuiHandler)
		v_u_1.Parent.Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1
			v_u_1.Visible = true
		end)
		v_u_1.CloseButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1
			v_u_1.Visible = false
		end)
		v_u_6.PrepareInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p30, p31, p32)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_9
			print(p32 .. " PREPARE INVENTORY")
			if p32 == "WEAPONS" then
				print("Weapons")
				v_u_18(p30, p31, "WEAPONS")
				for _, v33 in pairs(p31) do
					print("I have " .. v33)
				end
				for _, v34 in pairs(p31) do
					print("Doing for weapon " .. v34)
					v_u_9.AddToInventory(v34, p31, p32)
				end
			elseif p32 == "TITLES" then
				v_u_18(p30, p31, p32)
				for _, v35 in pairs(p31) do
					v_u_9.AddToInventory(v35, p31, "TITLES")
				end
			end
		end)
		v_u_6.AddToInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p36, p37)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9
			v_u_9.AddToInventory(p36, nil, p37)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_22
			while #v_u_2:GetChildren() < 10 do
				task.wait(1)
			end
			game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Equipped"):Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_22
				v_u_22()
			end)
			v_u_22()
		end)
	end
end
return v_u_9

local v4 = {}

function v4.Init(p6, p7, p8) -- name: Init
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_1
	if p6 then
		v_u_5 = p6
	end
	local v_u_9 = {
		["Void Blade"] = v_u_5,
		["Sapphire Dragon"] = p8,
		["Hellfire Edge"] = p7
	}
	local v_u_10 = { "rbxassetid://101782503367735", "rbxassetid://106548445029752", "rbxassetid://115877170881973" }
	task.spawn(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_10
		v_u_3:PreloadAsync(v_u_10)
		print("Reward images preloaded!")
	end)
	v_u_2.Remotes.PlayRewardFrame.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p11)
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_1
		local v_u_12 = v_u_9[p11]
		if v_u_12 then
			local v_u_13 = v_u_12:FindFirstChild("UIScale") or Instance.new("UIScale")
			v_u_13.Parent = v_u_12
			v_u_13.Scale = 0
			v_u_12.Visible = true
			v_u_1:Create(v_u_13, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
				["Scale"] = 1
			}):Play()
			task.delay(3, function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_12
				local v14 = v_u_1:Create(v_u_13, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
					["Scale"] = 0
				})
				v14:Play()
				v14.Completed:Once(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12
					v_u_12.Visible = false
				end)
			end)
		end
	end)
end
return v4

			local v29 = v28.Name:lower()

local function v_u_32(p31) -- name: ResetSelections
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_26, (ref) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_15
	if #v_u_26 > 0 then
		v_u_26[1]:Stop()
		v_u_26[2].Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
		v_u_26 = {}
	end
	if v_u_21 and v_u_21:FindFirstChild("RedSelected") then
		v_u_21.RedSelected.Visible = false
		v_u_21.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	end
	if v_u_22 and v_u_22:FindFirstChild("BlueSelected") then
		v_u_22.BlueSelected.Visible = false
		v_u_22.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	end
	v_u_21 = nil
	v_u_22 = nil
	v_u_20 = true
	v_u_19 = false
	if v_u_15 then
		v_u_15.Visible = false
	end
	if p31 then
		p31.Visible = true
	end
end
function v_u_1.Fill() -- name: Fill
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_26, (ref) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_15
	local v33 = v_u_7.Template
	for _, v_u_34 in ipairs(game.Workspace.Songs:GetChildren()) do
		local v_u_35 = v33:Clone()
		v_u_35.Name = v_u_34.Name
		v_u_35.Frame.Image.Image = v_u_34.Decal.ColorMap
		v_u_35.Frame.NameLabel.Text = v_u_34.Name
		v_u_35.Parent = v_u_7
		v_u_35.Visible = true
		if v_u_35:FindFirstChild("RedSelected") then
			v_u_35.RedSelected.Visible = false
		end
		if v_u_35:FindFirstChild("BlueSelected") then
			v_u_35.BlueSelected.Visible = false
		end
		v_u_35.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_35, (ref) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_15
			if #v_u_26 > 0 then
				v_u_26[1]:Stop()
				v_u_26[2].Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
			end
			if v_u_34 then
				v_u_34.TimePosition = 0
				v_u_34:Play()
				v_u_26 = { v_u_34, v_u_35 }
			end
			v_u_35.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0, 1, 0)
			if v_u_19 then
				if v_u_20 then
					if v_u_22 == v_u_35 then
						print("This song is already selected for the Blue team!")
						return
					end
					if v_u_21 and v_u_21:FindFirstChild("RedSelected") then
						v_u_21.RedSelected.Visible = false
						v_u_21.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					end
					v_u_21 = v_u_35
					v_u_35.RedSelected.Visible = true
					v_u_20 = false
				else
					if v_u_21 == v_u_35 then
						print("This song is already selected for the Red team!")
						return
					end
					if v_u_22 and v_u_22:FindFirstChild("BlueSelected") then
						v_u_22.BlueSelected.Visible = false
						v_u_22.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					end
					v_u_22 = v_u_35
					v_u_35.BlueSelected.Visible = true
					v_u_20 = true
				end
				if v_u_21 and (v_u_22 and v_u_15) then
					v_u_15.Visible = true
				end
			end
		end)
	end
end

local v_u_1 = {}

function v_u_1.ThrowUI(p7) -- name: ThrowUI
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6
	local v8 = v_u_3
	v8.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("IsVip") and "+$50 For Winning" or "+$25 For Winning"
	if p7 then
		v8 = v_u_4
		v8.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("IsVip") and "+$60 For Killing Player" or "+$30 For Killing Player"
	end
	local v9 = v8:Clone()
	v9.Parent = v_u_2.Parent
	v9.Visible = true
	v_u_5:Create(v9, v_u_6, {
		["Position"] = nil,
		["TextTransparency"] = 1,
		["Position"] = UDim2.new(v9.Position.X.Scale, 0, v9.Position.Y.Scale - 0.4, 0)
	}):Play()
	local v_u_10 = game.SoundService["Cash Earned"]:Clone()
	v_u_10.Parent = game.SoundService.Temp
	v_u_10:Play()
	v_u_10.Ended:Once(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10
		v_u_10:Destroy()
	end)
end
function v_u_1.Start(p11) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_1
	v_u_2 = p11
	v_u_3 = v_u_2.Parent:WaitForChild("GameWon")
	v_u_4 = v_u_2.Parent:WaitForChild("PlayerKilled")
	local v_u_12 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local v_u_13 = 0
	local v_u_14 = true
	local function v_u_21(p15) -- name: HandleCash
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12, (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_14
		if not v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash") then
			return
		end
		local v16 = v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash")
		if not p15 then
			local v17 = v_u_13 - v16
			if math.abs(v17) ~= 30 then
				local v18 = v_u_13 - v16
				if math.abs(v18) ~= 60 then
					local v19 = v_u_13 - v16
					if math.abs(v19) ~= 25 then
						local v20 = v_u_13 - v16
						if math.abs(v20) ~= 50 then
							goto l4
						end
					end
					v_u_1.ThrowUI(false)
					goto l4
				end
			end
			v_u_1.ThrowUI(true)
		end
		::l4::
		v_u_13 = v16
		v_u_2.Cash.Text = "$" .. v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash")
		v_u_14 = false
	end
	v_u_12:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Cash"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_14
		v_u_21(v_u_14)
	end)
	v_u_21(v_u_14)
end
return v_u_1

function v1.Start() -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2
	local v4 = v_u_2.Options.Music.Plus
	local v5 = v_u_2.Options.Music.Minus
	local v6 = v_u_2.Options.SFX.Plus
	local v7 = v_u_2.Options.SFX.Minus
	local v_u_8 = v_u_2.Options.Music.Value
	local v_u_9 = v_u_2.Options.SFX.Value
	local v_u_10 = v_u_2.Options.Hitbox.Button
	local function v_u_13(p11) -- name: SFXVolumeChange
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9
		for _, v12 in ipairs(game.SoundService:GetDescendants()) do
			if v12:IsA("Sound") and v12.Name ~= "Theme" then
				v12.Volume = p11 / 100
			end
		end
		v_u_9.Vol.Text = p11 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	end
	local v_u_14 = 50
	local v_u_15 = 50
	local v16 = v_u_15
	game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v16 / 100
	v_u_8.Vol.Text = v16 .. "%"
	game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	v_u_13(v_u_14)
	v4.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_8
		local v17 = v_u_15 + 5
		v_u_15 = math.clamp(v17, 0, 100)
		local v18 = v_u_15
		game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v18 / 100
		v_u_8.Vol.Text = v18 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	end)
	v5.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_8
		local v19 = v_u_15 - 5
		v_u_15 = math.clamp(v19, 0, 100)
		local v20 = v_u_15
		game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v20 / 100
		v_u_8.Vol.Text = v20 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	end)
	v6.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_13
		local v21 = v_u_14 + 5
		v_u_14 = math.clamp(v21, 0, 100)
		v_u_13(v_u_14)
	end)
	v7.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_13
		local v22 = v_u_14 - 5
		v_u_14 = math.clamp(v22, 0, 100)
		v_u_13(v_u_14)
	end)
	local v_u_23 = false
	for _, v24 in ipairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
		if v24.Character and v24.Character:WaitForChild("HitBox") then
			v24.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 1
		end
	end
	game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(p_u_25)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23
		p_u_25.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_25, (ref) v_u_23
			if p_u_25.Character and p_u_25.Character:WaitForChild("HitBox") then
				if v_u_23 then
					p_u_25.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 0.999
					return
				end
				p_u_25.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 1
			end
		end)
	end)
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(p26)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23

			if v_u_23 then

				return
			end
			p26.HitBox.Transparency = 1
		end
	end)
	v_u_10.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_10
		if game.ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GameState") and game.ReplicatedStorage.GameState:GetAttribute("Status") == "Choosing" then
			return
		else
			game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
			if v_u_23 then
				v_u_10.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
				v_u_23 = false
				v_u_10.Text = "Off"
				game.ReplicatedStorage.HitBox.Transparency = 1
				for _, v27 in ipairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
					v27.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 1
				end
			else
				v_u_10.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
				v_u_23 = true
				v_u_10.Text = "On"
				game.ReplicatedStorage.HitBox.Transparency = 0.999
				for _, v28 in ipairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
					v28.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 0.999
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end

local v1 = {}

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes")
local v_u_3 = nil
local v_u_4 = nil
local v_u_5 = nil
local v_u_6 = {}
local v_u_7 = {}
function v1.Start() -- name: Start end
function v1.Init(p8, p9) -- name: Init
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_7
	v_u_3 = p8
	v_u_5 = p9
	if not v_u_3:FindFirstChild("Products") then
		task.wait(1)
		print("Trying to find Products")
	end
	v_u_4 = v_u_3:FindFirstChild("Products")
	for _, v10 in ipairs(v_u_4:GetChildren()) do
		if v10:IsA("Frame") then
			local v_u_11 = v10:WaitForChild("Buy")
			v_u_6[string.upper(v10.Name)] = v10
			print(v_u_11.Name .. "FOUND IN PRODUCTS")
			local v_u_12 = v_u_11:GetAttribute("ProductId")
			if v_u_12 then
				v_u_11.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
					local v13, v14 = pcall(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_12
						v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(game.Players.LocalPlayer, v_u_12)
					end)
					if not v13 then
						warn("Error while purchasing " .. v_u_11.Name .. ": " .. v14)
					end
				end)
			else
				warn("ProductId not found for " .. v_u_11.Name)
			end
		end
	end
	v_u_2.promptProductPurchaseFinished:Connect(function(p15, p16, p17)
		if p15 == game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId and p17 then
			print("Purchase Sucess for productId " .. p16)
		end
	end)
	local v_u_18 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local function v_u_23(p19) -- name: ProduceFrame
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5
		if p19 == "RAGE" or p19 == "ELECTRIC" then
			local v_u_20 = v_u_5:FindFirstChild(p19)
			if v_u_20 then
				v_u_20 = v_u_20:Clone()
			end
			v_u_20.Parent = v_u_5
			local v_u_21 = p19 == "RAGE" and 60 or 90
			v_u_20.Time.Text = v_u_21 .. "s"
			local function v22() -- name: UpdateTime
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_21
				while v_u_20 and v_u_20.Parent do
					if game.ReplicatedStorage.GameState:GetAttribute("Status") ~= "Fight" then
						v_u_20:Destroy()
						return
					end
					if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Team == game.Teams.Lobby then
						v_u_20:Destroy()
						return
					end
					if v_u_20 and v_u_20.Parent then
						if v_u_21 <= 0 then
							v_u_20:Destroy()
							return
						end
						v_u_21 = v_u_21 - 1
						v_u_20.Time.Text = v_u_21 .. "s"
					end
					task.wait(1)
				end
			end
			v_u_20.Visible = true
			v22()
		end
	end
	local function v_u_26(p24) -- name: UpdatePotion
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_23
		if v_u_18:GetAttribute(p24) then
			v_u_6[p24].Own.Text = "Own: " .. v_u_18:GetAttribute(p24) .. "x"

				v_u_7[p24] = 0
				v25 = 0
			end
			v_u_7[p24] = v_u_18:GetAttribute(p24)
			if v25 and v_u_7[p24] < v25 then
				v_u_23(string.upper(p24))
			end
		end
	end
	for v_u_27, _ in pairs(v_u_6) do
		v_u_26(v_u_27)
		game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal(v_u_27):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_27
			v_u_26(v_u_27)
		end)
	end
	print("POTION HANDLER: DONE SETTING POTIONS")
end
return v1

local v1 = {}
local v_u_2 = nil
local v_u_3 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes")
local v_u_4 = nil
function v1.Init(p5) -- name: Init
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3
	v_u_2 = p5
	for _, v_u_6 in ipairs(v_u_2.Titles.TitlesFrame:GetChildren()) do
		if v_u_6:IsA("Frame") then
			v_u_6.EquipButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
				if v_u_4 == v_u_6.EquipButton then
					v_u_3.Equip:FireServer("NONE", "TITLES")
				else
					v_u_3.Equip:FireServer(v_u_6.Name, "TITLES")
				end
			end)
		end
	end
	local function v_u_9() -- name: HandleChanged
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_2
		local v7 = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("EquippedTitle")
		if v7 then
			if v7 == "NONE" then
				if v_u_4 then
					v_u_4:FindFirstChild("TextLabel").Text = "Equip"
					v_u_4 = nil
				end
			else
				if v_u_4 then
					v_u_4:FindFirstChild("TextLabel").Text = "Equip"
					v_u_4 = nil
				end
				local v8 = v_u_2.Titles.TitlesFrame:FindFirstChild(v7)
				v8.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
				v_u_4 = v8.EquipButton
			end
		else
			return
		end
	end
	game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("EquippedTitle"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9
		v_u_9()
	end)
	v_u_9()
end
return v1

-- [ModuleScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.RewardHandler
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_2 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local v3 = {}
local v_u_4 = nil
function v3.Init(p5) -- name: Init
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_1
	if p5 then
		v_u_4 = p5
	end
	v_u_2.Remotes:WaitForChild("PlayRewardFrame").OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p6)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_1
		local v_u_7 = ({
			["Golden Royale"] = v_u_4,
			["Tornado Fan"] = v_u_4.Parent:FindFirstChild("TornadoFan_Reward_Frame"),
			["Shadow King"] = v_u_4.Parent:FindFirstChild("ShadowKing_Reward_Frame"),
			["Griffin"] = v_u_4.Parent:FindFirstChild("Griffin_Reward_Frame")
		})[p6]
		if v_u_7 then
			game.SoundService["VIP Weapon Reward"]:Play()
			local v_u_8 = v_u_7:FindFirstChild("UIScale")
			if not v_u_8 then
				v_u_8 = Instance.new("UIScale")
				v_u_8.Parent = v_u_7
			end
			v_u_8.Scale = 0
			v_u_7.Visible = true
			v_u_1:Create(v_u_8, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
				["Scale"] = 1
			}):Play()
			task.delay(3, function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_7
				local v9 = v_u_1:Create(v_u_8, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
					["Scale"] = 0
				})
				v9:Play()
				v9.Completed:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7
					v_u_7.Visible = false
				end)
			end)
		end
	end)
end
return v3

	v_u_5.RichText = true
	if v6 then
		local v9 = v6.Team == game.Teams.Red and v7 and v7 or v8
		if v6.Team == game.Teams.Red then
			v7 = v8 or v7
		end

		v_u_5.Text = string.format("<font color=\"%s\">%s</font> Eliminated <font color=\"%s\">%s</font>", v10, p4.player1, v11, p4.player2)
	end

		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5

			v_u_10.Visible = true

			return nil
		end
		local v19 = v17 + (v_u_11[v18[3]] - v17) % 360 + 7200
		local v20 = game:GetService("TweenService")
		local v21 = TweenInfo.new(9, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)

			["Rotation"] = v19
		})
		v22:Play()

		if v18[4] == "WEAPONS" then
			game.SoundService["Mythical Summon"]:Play()
			local v23 = "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'>[Server Announcement]: " .. game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. " Spinned A </font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FF0000" .. "\'>" .. "Mythical" .. "</font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'> Weapon " .. v18[1] .. "</font>"
			if game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Announce") then
				game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Announce:FireServer(v23)
			end
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_8, v18[1], v18[2])
		else
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_7, v18[1], v18[2])
		end
		v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("REWARD")
		v_u_9 = true
		v_u_10.Visible = true
	end
end

local v_u_2 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local _ = v_u_2.PlayerGui

local v_u_4 = nil

local v_u_6 = nil
local v_u_7 = nil
local v_u_8 = nil
local v_u_9 = nil
local v_u_10 = nil
local v_u_11 = {}
local function v_u_14(p12, p13) -- name: Unlock
	if p13 and p13 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p13 == "TITLES" then
			if p12:FindFirstChild("LockedButton") then
				p12.LockedButton.Visible = false
			end
			if p12:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
				p12.EquipButton.Visible = true
			end
		end
		return
	elseif p12 then
		p12.WeaponImage.Transparency = 0
		p12.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
		if p12.WeaponImage:FindFirstChild("Locked") then
			p12.WeaponImage.Locked.Visible = false
		end
		p12.EquipButton.Visible = true
		p12.LockedButton.Visible = false
	end
end
local function v_u_34(p15, p16, p17) -- name: PrepareInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_8
	if p15 then
		task.defer(function()
			EquipWeapon()
		end)
		if p17 == "TITLES" then
			for _, v18 in pairs(p15.Titles) do
				local v19 = v_u_7:FindFirstChild(v18.Name)
				if v19 and table.find(p16, v18.Name) then
					v_u_14(v19, p17)
				end
			end
		else
			local v20 = v_u_9.Samples
			local v21 = {}
			for _, v22 in pairs(p16 or {}) do
				v21[v22] = true
			end
			for _, v23 in ipairs(v_u_4:GetChildren()) do
				if v23:IsA("Frame") and v23 ~= v_u_4.WeaponTemplate then
					v23:Destroy()
				end
			end
			for _, v_u_24 in pairs(p15.Weapons) do
				local v_u_25 = v_u_4.WeaponTemplate.TemplateLocked:Clone()
				v_u_25.Name = v_u_24.weaponName
				v_u_25.Parent = v_u_4
				v_u_25.Visible = true
				v_u_25.WeaponImage.Image.Image = v_u_24.image
				v_u_25.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
				v_u_25.WeaponName.Text = v_u_24.weaponName
				v_u_25.Rarity.Text = v_u_24.rarity
				local v26 = v20[v_u_24.rarity]
				if v26 then
					v_u_25.UIGradient.Color = v26.Gradient
					v_u_25.WeaponImage.Stroke.BackgroundColor3 = v26.Color
				end
				if v_u_24.rarity == "Limited" and v26 then
					v_u_25.WeaponName.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					v_u_25.Rarity.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					local v_u_27 = -1
					local v_u_28 = {}
					for _, v29 in pairs({ v_u_25.WeaponName, v_u_25.Rarity }) do
						local v30 = Instance.new("UIGradient")
						v30.Color = v26.Gradient
						v30.Offset = Vector2.new(v_u_27, 0)
						v30.Parent = v29
						table.insert(v_u_28, v30)
					end
					local v_u_31 = nil
					v_u_31 = v_u_1.Heartbeat:Connect(function(p32)
						-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_25, (ref) v_u_31, (ref) v_u_27, (copy) v_u_28
						if v_u_25.Parent then
							v_u_27 = v_u_27 + p32 * 1
							if v_u_27 >= 1 then
								v_u_27 = -1
							end
							for _, v33 in ipairs(v_u_28) do
								v33.Offset = Vector2.new(v_u_27, 0)
							end
						else
							v_u_31:Disconnect()
						end
					end)
				elseif v26 then
					v_u_25.WeaponName.TextColor3 = v26.Color
					v_u_25.Rarity.TextColor3 = v26.Color
				end
				if v21[v_u_24.weaponName] then
					print("UNLOCKING:", v_u_24.weaponName)
					if v_u_25 then
						v_u_25.WeaponImage.Transparency = 0
						v_u_25.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
						if v_u_25.WeaponImage:FindFirstChild("Locked") then
							v_u_25.WeaponImage.Locked.Visible = false
						end
						v_u_25.EquipButton.Visible = true
						v_u_25.LockedButton.Visible = false
					end
				end
				v_u_25.EquipButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_24
					game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
					v_u_8.EquipWeapon:FireServer(v_u_24.weaponName)
				end)
			end
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
function EquipWeapon() -- name: EquipWeapon
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_10
	local v35 = v_u_2:GetAttribute("Equipped") or "Baseball Bat"
	for _, v36 in ipairs(v_u_4:GetChildren()) do
		if v36:IsA("Frame") and v36:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
			v36.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equip"
		end
	end
	print("Children count:", #v_u_4:GetChildren())
	local v37 = v_u_4:FindFirstChild(v35)
	if v37 and v37:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
		v37.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
		v_u_10 = v37.EquipButton
		print("Equipped set to:", v35)
	else
		warn("Could not find frame for equipped weapon:", v35)
	end
end
function v_u_11.AddToInventory(p38, _, p39) -- name: AddToInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_7
	if p39 and p39 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p39 == "TITLES" then
			print("TRYING TO FIND FRAME FOR " .. p38)
			local v40 = v_u_7:WaitForChild(p38, (1 / 0))
			if v40 then
				v_u_14(v40, p39)
			end
			print("FOUND AND UNLOCK " .. p38)
		end
		return
	else
		local v41 = v_u_4:WaitForChild(p38, (1 / 0))
		if v41 then
			v_u_14(v41, p39)
		else
			warn("Could not find frame for weapon:", p38)
		end
	end
end
function v_u_11.Start(p42, p43) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_11
	v_u_3 = p42
	v_u_4 = v_u_3.Weapon.OutnerFrame.Weapons.InnerFrameLayout
	v_u_5 = p43
	v_u_6 = v_u_5.Titles
	v_u_7 = v_u_6.TitlesFrame
	v_u_8 = game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes
	v_u_9 = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponDatabase)
	v_u_10 = nil
	if v_u_3 then
		require(game.ReplicatedStorage.MainGuiHandler)
		v_u_3.Parent.Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3
			v_u_3.Visible = true
		end)
		v_u_3.CloseButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3
			v_u_3.Visible = false
		end)
		v_u_8.PrepareInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p44, p45, p46)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_34
			print(p46 .. " PREPARE INVENTORY")
			if p46 == "WEAPONS" then
				print("Weapons")
				v_u_34(p44, p45, "WEAPONS")
			elseif p46 == "TITLES" then
				v_u_34(p44, p45, p46)
			end
		end)
		v_u_8.AddToInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p47, p48)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_11
			v_u_11.AddToInventory(p47, nil, p48)
		end)
		game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Equipped"):Connect(function()
			EquipWeapon()
		end)
	end
end
return v_u_11

	["CYCLES"] = 20,
	["SPIN_TIME"] = 11,
	["WINNING_INDEX_OFFSET"] = 40,
	["RESET_DELAY"] = 1.5,
	["RARITY_DISTRIBUTION"] = nil,
	["RARITY_DISTRIBUTION"] = {
		["Common"] = -2,
		["Rare"] = -2,
		["Epic"] = 60,
		["Legendary"] = 30,
		["Mythical"] = 10,
		["Exclusive"] = 1
	}

local function v_u_33(p27) -- name: ShuffleTable
	local v28 = Random.new()
	for v29 = #p27, 2, -1 do
		local v30 = v28:NextInteger(1, v29)
		local v31 = p27[v30]
		local v32 = p27[v29]
		p27[v29] = v31
		p27[v30] = v32
	end
	return p27
end
local function v_u_36(p34) -- name: GetWeaponData
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7
	for _, v35 in pairs(v_u_7.Weapons) do
		if v35.weaponName == p34 then
			return { v35, v_u_7.Samples[v35.rarity] }
		end
	end
	warn("Weapon not found:", p34)
	return nil
end
function v_u_6.RecalculateMetrics() -- name: RecalculateMetrics
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_19, (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_23
	local v37 = 1 / (v_u_19.X.Scale + 0.01)
	local v38 = math.floor(v37)
	local v39 = UDim2.new(v_u_22.X.Scale * v_u_5.CYCLES, 0, v_u_22.Y.Scale, 0)
	local v40 = v_u_19.X.Scale / v_u_5.CYCLES
	local v41 = v_u_20.X.Scale / v_u_5.CYCLES
	local v42 = v38 * v_u_5.CYCLES
	v_u_23 = {
		["BeltSize"] = v39,
		["CellSize"] = UDim2.new(v40, 0, v_u_19.Y.Scale, 0),
		["CellPadding"] = UDim2.new(v41, 0, 0, 0),
		["TotalCells"] = v42,
		["SlotWidth"] = v_u_19.X.Scale + v_u_20.X.Scale
	}
end
function v_u_6.ResetBelt() -- name: ResetBelt
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_12
	if not v_u_23.BeltSize then
		v_u_6.RecalculateMetrics()
	end
	v_u_11.Size = v_u_23.BeltSize
	v_u_11.Position = v_u_21
	v_u_13.CellSize = v_u_23.CellSize
	v_u_13.CellPadding = v_u_23.CellPadding
	for _, v43 in ipairs(v_u_11:GetChildren()) do
		if v43:IsA("Frame") and v43 ~= v_u_12 then
			v43:Destroy()
		end
	end
end
function v_u_6.PopulateBelt() -- name: PopulateBelt
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
	local v44 = {
		["Common"] = {},
		["Rare"] = {},
		["Epic"] = {},
		["Legendary"] = {},
		["Mythical"] = {},
		["Exclusive"] = {}
	}
	for _, v45 in pairs(v_u_7.Weapons) do
		if v45.weaponName ~= "Baseball Bat" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Frozen Blade" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Golden Royale" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Griffin" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Tornado Fan" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Shadow King" and v44[v45.rarity]))))) then
			local v46 = v44[v45.rarity]
			local v47 = { v45.weaponName, v45.image }
			table.insert(v46, v47)
		end
	end
	local v48 = v_u_23.TotalCells
	local v49 = 0
	local v50 = {}
	for v51, v52 in pairs(v_u_5.RARITY_DISTRIBUTION) do
		local v53 = v52 * v48 / 100
		local v54 = math.floor(v53)
		local v55 = v44[v51]
		if v55 and #v55 ~= 0 then
			for _ = 1, v54 + 1 do
				if v48 <= v49 then
					break
				end
				v49 = v49 + 1
				local v56 = v55[math.random(1, #v55)]
				local v57 = {
					["Rarity"] = v51,
					["Name"] = v56[1],
					["Image"] = v56[2]
				}
				table.insert(v50, v57)
			end
		end
	end
	v_u_33(v50)
	for v58, v59 in ipairs(v50) do
		local v60 = (v_u_12:FindFirstChild(v59.Rarity) or v_u_12:FindFirstChild("Common")):Clone()
		v60.Name = tostring(v58)
		v60["Weapon Name"].Text = v59.Name
		v60.Image.Image = v59.Image
		v60.Visible = true
		v60.Parent = v_u_11
	end
end
function v_u_6.SetWinningTile(p61) -- name: SetWinningTile
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_36, (copy) v_u_12
	local v62 = v_u_23.TotalCells - v_u_5.WINNING_INDEX_OFFSET
	local v63 = v_u_11:FindFirstChild((tostring(v62)))
	v_u_14.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	if not v63 then
		return warn("Winning frame index not found")
	end
	local v64 = v_u_36(p61)
	if v64 then
		local v65 = v_u_12:FindFirstChild(v64[1].rarity) or v_u_12:FindFirstChild("Common")
		v63["Weapon Name"].Text = p61
		v63.Image.Image = v64[1].image
		v63.UIGradient.Color = v65.UIGradient.Color
		v63.UIStroke.Color = v65.UIStroke.Color
		v_u_14.Image.Image = v64[1].image
		v_u_14["Weapon Name"].Text = p61
		v_u_14.UIGradient.Color = v65.UIGradient.Color
		v_u_14.UIStroke.Color = v65.UIStroke.Color
		v_u_14.Rarities.Text = v64[1].rarity
		v_u_14.Rarities.TextColor3 = v64[2].Color
	end
	return v63
end
function v_u_6.AnimateSpin(p66) -- name: AnimateSpin
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_17
	if p66 then
		local v67 = p66.Name
		local v68 = -(tonumber(v67) - 1) * v_u_23.SlotWidth + 0.5 - v_u_19.X.Scale / 2
		v_u_26 = UDim2.new(v68, 0, v_u_21.Y.Scale, 0)
		task.wait(0.1)
		local v69 = {
			["Position"] = v_u_26
		}
		v_u_25 = v_u_3:Create(v_u_11, TweenInfo.new(v_u_5.SPIN_TIME, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), v69)
		if game.SoundService:FindFirstChild("Spinning Sound") then
			game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Play()
		end
		v_u_17.Visible = true
		v_u_25:Play()
		v_u_25.Completed:Wait()
		if game.SoundService:FindFirstChild("Spinning Sound") then
			game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Stop()
		end
		print("Spin done")
		v_u_17.Visible = false
	end
end
function v_u_6.RunSpin(p70, p71) -- name: RunSpin
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_24
	local v72 = v_u_6.SetWinningTile(p70)
	v_u_6.AnimateSpin(v72)
	if v_u_14.Rarities.Text == "Mythical" then
		game.SoundService["Mythical Summon"]:Play()
		local v73 = "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'>[Server Announcement]: " .. game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. " Summoned A </font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FF0000" .. "\'>" .. "Mythical" .. "</font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'> Weapon " .. p70 .. "</font>"
		if game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Announce") then
			game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Announce:FireServer(v73)
		end
	else
		game.SoundService["Summoned Sound"]:Play()
	end
	local v74
	if p71 then
		v74 = v_u_15.Parent.Refund:Clone()
		v74.Parent = v_u_15.Parent
		v74.Visible = true
	else
		v74 = nil
	end
	v_u_14.Visible = true
	v_u_3:Create(v_u_14, TweenInfo.new(0.175, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		["Size"] = UDim2.new(0.4, 0, 0.4, 0)
	}):Play()
	task.wait(0.5)
	task.wait(v_u_5.RESET_DELAY)
	task.wait(0.5)
	v_u_6.ResetBelt()
	v_u_6.PopulateBelt()
	v_u_14.Visible = false
	if v74 then
		v74:Destroy()
	end
	v_u_15.Visible = true
	v_u_16.Visible = true
	v_u_18.Visible = true
	v_u_24 = false
end
function v_u_6.Start() -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
	local v75 = v_u_9:GetAttribute("MythicalSpins") or 0
	v_u_16.TextLabel.Text = "Spin Amount: " .. v75
	v_u_9:GetAttributeChangedSignal("MythicalSpins"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_16
		local v76 = v_u_9:GetAttribute("MythicalSpins") or 0
		v_u_16.TextLabel.Text = "Spin Amount: " .. v76
	end)
	require(v_u_1.MainGuiHandler)
	v_u_17.Visible = false
	v_u_6.ResetBelt()
	v_u_6.PopulateBelt()
	v_u_15.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
		if not v_u_24 then
			v_u_24 = true
			local v77, v78 = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
				v_u_4:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, 3506187073)
			end)
			if not v77 then
				warn("Purchase Prompt Failed: " .. tostring(v78))
				v_u_24 = false
			end
		end
	end)
	v_u_16.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_8
		if v_u_24 then
			return
		elseif (v_u_9:GetAttribute("MythicalSpins") or 0) > 0 then
			v_u_24 = true
			v_u_8.RequestFreeMythicalSpin:FireServer()
		end
	end)
	v_u_4.PromptProductPurchaseFinished:Connect(function(p79, _, p80)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_24
		if p79 == v_u_9.UserId and not p80 then
			v_u_24 = false
		end
	end)
	if v_u_8:FindFirstChild("RobuxMyhicalSpinResult") then
		v_u_8.RobuxMyhicalSpinResult.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p81, p82)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_6
			v_u_24 = false
			if p81 then
				v_u_15.Visible = false
				v_u_16.Visible = false
				v_u_18.Visible = false
				v_u_6.RunSpin(p81, p82)
			end
		end)
	end
	v_u_17.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_25, (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
		if v_u_25 and game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("isFastSpin") then
			v_u_25:Cancel()
			v_u_11.Position = v_u_26 or UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
		end
	end)
end
return v_u_6

	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_12

		v_u_6.RecalculateMetrics()

	v_u_11.Size = v_u_23.BeltSize

function v_u_6.PopulateBelt() -- name: PopulateBelt
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
	local v44 = {
		["Common"] = {},
		["Rare"] = {},
		["Epic"] = {},
		["Legendary"] = {},
		["Mythical"] = {},
		["Exclusive"] = {}
	}
	for _, v45 in pairs(v_u_7.Weapons) do
		if v45.weaponName ~= "Baseball Bat" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Frozen Blade" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Golden Royale" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Griffin" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Tornado Fan" and (v45.weaponName ~= "Shadow King" and v44[v45.rarity]))))) then
			local v46 = v44[v45.rarity]
			local v47 = { v45.weaponName, v45.image }
			table.insert(v46, v47)
		end
	end
	local v48 = v_u_23.TotalCells
	local v49 = 0
	local v50 = {}
	for v51, v52 in pairs(v_u_5.RARITY_DISTRIBUTION) do
		local v53 = v52 * v48 / 100
		local v54 = math.floor(v53)
		local v55 = v44[v51]
		if v55 and #v55 ~= 0 then
			for _ = 1, v54 + 1 do
				if v48 <= v49 then
					break
				end
				v49 = v49 + 1
				local v56 = v55[math.random(1, #v55)]
				local v57 = {
					["Rarity"] = v51,
					["Name"] = v56[1],
					["Image"] = v56[2]
				}
				table.insert(v50, v57)
			end
		end
	end
	v_u_33(v50)
	for v58, v59 in ipairs(v50) do
		local v60 = (v_u_12:FindFirstChild(v59.Rarity) or v_u_12:FindFirstChild("Common")):Clone()
		v60.Name = tostring(v58)
		v60["Weapon Name"].Text = v59.Name
		v60.Image.Image = v59.Image
		v60.Visible = true
		v60.Parent = v_u_11
	end
end
function v_u_6.SetWinningTile(p61) -- name: SetWinningTile

	local v62 = v_u_23.TotalCells - v_u_5.WINNING_INDEX_OFFSET
	local v63 = v_u_11:FindFirstChild((tostring(v62)))
	v_u_14.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)

		v_u_14.UIStroke.Color = v65.UIStroke.Color

function v_u_6.AnimateSpin(p66) -- name: AnimateSpin
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_17
	if p66 then
		local v67 = p66.Name
		local v68 = -(tonumber(v67) - 1) * v_u_23.SlotWidth + 0.5 - v_u_19.X.Scale / 2
		v_u_26 = UDim2.new(v68, 0, v_u_21.Y.Scale, 0)
		task.wait(0.1)
		local v69 = {
			["Position"] = v_u_26
		}
		v_u_25 = v_u_3:Create(v_u_11, TweenInfo.new(v_u_5.SPIN_TIME, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), v69)
		if game.SoundService:FindFirstChild("Spinning Sound") then
			game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Play()
		end
		v_u_17.Visible = true
		v_u_25:Play()
		v_u_25.Completed:Wait()
		if game.SoundService:FindFirstChild("Spinning Sound") then
			game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Stop()
		end

		v_u_17.Visible = false

end
function v_u_6.RunSpin(p70, p71) -- name: RunSpin
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_24
	local v72 = v_u_6.SetWinningTile(p70)
	v_u_6.AnimateSpin(v72)
	if v_u_14.Rarities.Text == "Exclusive" then
		game.SoundService["Mythical Summon"]:Play()
		local v73 = "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'>[Server Announcement]: " .. game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. " Summoned A </font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#323232" .. "\'>" .. "Exclusive" .. "</font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'> Weapon " .. p70 .. "</font>"
		if game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Announce") then
			game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Announce:FireServer(v73)
		end
	else
		game.SoundService["Summoned Sound"]:Play()
	end
	local v74
	if p71 then
		v74 = v_u_15.Parent.Refund:Clone()
		v74.Parent = v_u_15.Parent
		v74.Visible = true
	else
		v74 = nil
	end
	v_u_14.Visible = true
	v_u_3:Create(v_u_14, TweenInfo.new(0.175, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		["Size"] = UDim2.new(0.4, 0, 0.4, 0)
	}):Play()
	task.wait(0.5)
	task.wait(v_u_5.RESET_DELAY)
	task.wait(0.5)
	v_u_6.ResetBelt()
	v_u_6.PopulateBelt()
	v_u_14.Visible = false
	if v74 then
		v74:Destroy()
	end
	v_u_15.Visible = true
	v_u_16.Visible = true
	v_u_18.Visible = true
	v_u_24 = false
end
function v_u_6.Start() -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
	local v75 = v_u_9:GetAttribute("ExclusiveSpins") or 0
	v_u_16.TextLabel.Text = "Spin Amount: " .. v75
	v_u_9:GetAttributeChangedSignal("ExclusiveSpins"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_16
		local v76 = v_u_9:GetAttribute("ExclusiveSpins") or 0
		v_u_16.TextLabel.Text = "Spin Amount: " .. v76
	end)
	require(v_u_1.MainGuiHandler)
	v_u_17.Visible = false
	v_u_6.ResetBelt()
	v_u_6.PopulateBelt()
	v_u_15.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
		if not v_u_24 then
			v_u_24 = true
			local v77, v78 = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
				v_u_4:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, 3534012488)
			end)
			if not v77 then
				warn("Purchase Prompt Failed: " .. tostring(v78))
				v_u_24 = false
			end
		end
	end)
	v_u_16.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_8
		if v_u_24 then
			return
		elseif (v_u_9:GetAttribute("ExclusiveSpins") or 0) > 0 then
			v_u_24 = true
			v_u_8.RequestFreeExclusiveSpin:FireServer()
		end
	end)
	v_u_4.PromptProductPurchaseFinished:Connect(function(p79, _, p80)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_24
		if p79 == v_u_9.UserId and not p80 then
			v_u_24 = false
		end
	end)
	if v_u_8:FindFirstChild("RobuxExclusiveSpinResult") then
		v_u_8.RobuxExclusiveSpinResult.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p81, p82)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_6
			v_u_24 = false
			if p81 then
				v_u_15.Visible = false
				v_u_16.Visible = false
				v_u_18.Visible = false
				v_u_6.RunSpin(p81, p82)
			end
		end)
	end
	v_u_17.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_25, (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
		if v_u_25 and game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("isFastSpin") then
			v_u_25:Cancel()
			v_u_11.Position = v_u_26 or UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
		end
	end)
end
return v_u_6

local function v_u_33(p27) -- name: ShuffleTable
	local v28 = Random.new()
	for v29 = #p27, 2, -1 do
		local v30 = v28:NextInteger(1, v29)
		local v31 = p27[v30]
		local v32 = p27[v29]
		p27[v29] = v31
		p27[v30] = v32
	end
	return p27
end

	local v37 = 1 / (v_u_19.X.Scale + 0.01)
	local v38 = math.floor(v37)
	local v39 = UDim2.new(v_u_22.X.Scale * v_u_5.CYCLES, 0, v_u_22.Y.Scale, 0)
	local v40 = v_u_19.X.Scale / v_u_5.CYCLES
	local v41 = v_u_20.X.Scale / v_u_5.CYCLES
	local v42 = v38 * v_u_5.CYCLES
	v_u_23 = {
		["BeltSize"] = v39,
		["CellSize"] = UDim2.new(v40, 0, v_u_19.Y.Scale, 0),

function v_u_6.Start() -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_25, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
	require(v_u_1.MainGuiHandler)
	v_u_17.Visible = false

	v_u_6.PopulateBelt()
	local function v_u_81() -- name: SpinButtonClicked
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_6
		if v_u_24 then
			return
		else
			v_u_24 = true
			local v77, v78 = v_u_8.InvokePurchase:InvokeServer(0)
			if v77 then
				v_u_16.Visible = false
				v_u_15.Visible = false
				v_u_18.Visible = false
				v_u_6.RunSpin(v77, v78, false)
			else
				v_u_24 = false
				task.spawn(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16
					local v79 = v_u_16.Parent:FindFirstChild("CashError")
					if v79 then
						local v80 = v79:Clone()
						v80.Parent = v_u_16.Parent
						v80.Visible = true
						game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Error:Play()
						task.wait(2)
						v80:Destroy()
					end
				end)
			end
		end
	end
	v_u_15.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_81
		v_u_81()
	end)
	v_u_16.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_24, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
		if not v_u_24 then
			v_u_24 = true
			local v82, v83 = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_9
				v_u_4:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, 3506186869)
			end)
			if not v82 then
				warn("Purchase Prompt Failed: " .. tostring(v83))
				v_u_24 = false
			end
		end
	end)
	v_u_4.PromptProductPurchaseFinished:Connect(function(p84, _, p85)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_24
		if p84 == v_u_9.UserId and not p85 then
			v_u_24 = false
		end
	end)
	if v_u_8:FindFirstChild("RobuxSpinResult") then
		v_u_8.RobuxSpinResult.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p86, p87)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_6
			if p86 then
				v_u_16.Visible = false
				v_u_15.Visible = false
				v_u_18.Visible = false
				v_u_6.RunSpin(p86, p87, true)
			end
		end)
	end
	v_u_17.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_25, (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_26
		if v_u_25 and game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("isFastSpin") then
			v_u_25:Cancel()
			v_u_11.Position = v_u_26 or UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
		end
	end)
end
return v_u_6

game:GetService("RunService")
local v_u_1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local _ = v_u_1.PlayerGui
local v_u_2 = nil
local v_u_3 = nil

local v_u_15 = ""
local v_u_16 = {}
local function v_u_22() -- name: UpdateVisibleWeapons
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_14
	for _, v17 in pairs(v_u_16) do
		if v17 and v17.Parent then
			local v18 = v17:GetAttribute("WeaponName") or ""
			local v19 = v17:GetAttribute("Rarity") or ""
			local v20 = v_u_15 == "" and true or string.find(string.lower(v18), string.lower(v_u_15), 1, true) ~= nil
			local v21 = (v_u_15 ~= "" or v_u_14 == "All") and true or v19 == v_u_14
			if string.find(v17.Name, "TEMPLATE_") then
				v17.Visible = false
			else
				v17.Visible = v20 and v21
			end
		end
	end
end
local function v_u_37(p23, p24, p25) -- name: PrepareInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_22
	if p25 == "TITLES" then
		for _, v26 in pairs(p23.Titles) do
			local v27 = v_u_9:FindFirstChild(v26.Name)
			if v27 and table.find(p24, v26.Name) then
				if v27:FindFirstChild("LockedButton") then
					v27.LockedButton.Visible = false
				end
				if v27:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
					v27.EquipButton.Visible = true
				end
			end
		end
	else
		v_u_16 = {}
		local v28 = {}
		for _, v29 in pairs(p24 or {}) do
			v28[v29] = true
		end
		for _, v30 in ipairs(v_u_3:GetChildren()) do
			if v30:IsA("Frame") and not string.find(v30.Name, "TEMPLATE_") then
				v30:Destroy()
			end
		end
		local v31 = #p23.Weapons
		local v32 = 0
		for _, v_u_33 in pairs(p23.Weapons) do
			local v34 = v_u_3:FindFirstChild("TEMPLATE_" .. v_u_33.rarity)
			if v34 then
				local v35 = v34:Clone()
				v35.Name = v_u_33.weaponName
				v35.Visible = true
				v35.Parent = v_u_3
				v35:SetAttribute("WeaponName", v_u_33.weaponName)
				v35:SetAttribute("Rarity", v_u_33.rarity)
				v35:WaitForChild("WeaponName").Text = v_u_33.weaponName
				v35:WaitForChild("Rarity").Text = v_u_33.rarity
				v35.WeaponIcon.Image = v_u_33.image
				v35["Equip/Unequip"]:WaitForChild("Text").Text = "Equip"
				if v28[v_u_33.weaponName] then
					v32 = v32 + 1
					if v35 then
						v35.WeaponIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
						v35.WeaponIcon.ImageTransparency = 0
						v35["Equip/Unequip"].Visible = true
						v35.Locked.Visible = false
					end
				else
					v35["Equip/Unequip"].Visible = false
					v35.Locked.Visible = true
					v35.WeaponIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
					v35.WeaponIcon.ImageTransparency = 0
				end
				v35["Equip/Unequip"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_33
					game:GetService("SoundService"):WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Hover"):Play()
					v_u_10.EquipWeapon:FireServer(v_u_33.weaponName)
				end)
				local v36 = v_u_16
				table.insert(v36, v35)
			else
				warn("Missing template for rarity:", v_u_33.rarity)
			end
		end
		v_u_6.Text = v32 .. "/" .. v31
		task.defer(function()
			EquipWeapon()
		end)
		v_u_22()
	end
end
function EquipWeapon() -- name: EquipWeapon
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_3
	local v38 = v_u_1:GetAttribute("Equipped") or "Baseball Bat"
	for _, v39 in pairs(v_u_16) do
		if v39:FindFirstChild("Equip/Unequip") then
			v39["Equip/Unequip"]:WaitForChild("Text").Text = "Equip"
		end
	end
	local v40 = v_u_3:FindFirstChild(v38)
	if v40 and v40:FindFirstChild("Equip/Unequip") then
		v40["Equip/Unequip"]:WaitForChild("Text").Text = "Equipped"
	end
end
function v_u_13.AddToInventory(p41, _, p42) -- name: AddToInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_9
	if p42 and p42 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p42 == "TITLES" then
			print("TRYING TO FIND FRAME FOR " .. p41)
			local v43 = v_u_9:WaitForChild(p41, (1 / 0))
			if v43 then
				if v43:FindFirstChild("LockedButton") then
					v43.LockedButton.Visible = false
				end
				if v43:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
					v43.EquipButton.Visible = true
				end
			end
			print("FOUND AND UNLOCK " .. p41)
		end
		return
	else
		local v44 = v_u_3:WaitForChild(p41, (1 / 0))
		if v44 then
			if v44 then
				v44.WeaponIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
				v44.WeaponIcon.ImageTransparency = 0
				v44["Equip/Unequip"].Visible = true
				v44.Locked.Visible = false
			end
		else
			warn("Could not find frame for weapon:", p41)
			return
		end
	end
end
function v_u_13.Start(p45, p46) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_12, (ref) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_37, (copy) v_u_13
	v_u_2 = p45
	v_u_3 = v_u_2.Background.WeaponFrame.ScrollingFrame
	v_u_4 = v_u_2.Background.WeaponFrame.Buttons.ScrollingFrame
	v_u_5 = v_u_2.Background["Unlocked & Search"].Search.TextBox
	v_u_6 = v_u_2.Background["Unlocked & Search"].Unlocked.Text
	v_u_7 = p46
	v_u_8 = v_u_7.Titles
	v_u_9 = v_u_8.TitlesFrame
	v_u_10 = game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes
	v_u_11 = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponDatabase)
	v_u_12 = nil
	if v_u_2 then
		require(game.ReplicatedStorage.MainGuiHandler)
		v_u_2.Parent.Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2
			v_u_2.Visible = true
			game:GetService("SoundService"):WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Open 2"):Play()
		end)
		v_u_5:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_15, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_22
			v_u_15 = v_u_5.Text
			v_u_22()
		end)
		for _, v_u_47 in pairs(v_u_4:GetChildren()) do
			if v_u_47:IsA("TextButton") then
				v_u_47.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_47, (ref) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_22
					game:GetService("SoundService"):WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Click 2"):Play()
					v_u_14 = v_u_47.Name:gsub("Button", "")
					v_u_22()
				end)
			end
		end
		v_u_10.PrepareInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p48, p49, p50)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_37
			print(p50 .. " PREPARE INVENTORY")
			if p50 == "WEAPONS" then
				print("Weapons")
				v_u_37(p48, p49, "WEAPONS")
			elseif p50 == "TITLES" then
				v_u_37(p48, p49, p50)
			end
		end)
		v_u_10.AddToInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p51, p52)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13
			v_u_13.AddToInventory(p51, nil, p52)
		end)
		game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Equipped"):Connect(function()
			EquipWeapon()
		end)
	end
end
return v_u_13

============================================================
-- [ModuleScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.SpinWheelHandler
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: InvokeServer, FireServer, Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v_u_1 = {}
local v_u_2 = nil
local v_u_3 = nil
local v_u_4 = nil
local v_u_5 = nil
local v_u_6 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes
local v_u_7 = nil
local v_u_8 = nil
local v_u_9 = true
local v_u_10 = nil
local v_u_11 = {
	["Orange"] = -75,
	["Yellow"] = -130,
	["Green"] = -180,
	["Blue"] = -230,
	["Purple"] = -285,
	["Magenta"] = -335,
	["Red"] = -385
}
function v_u_1.GetRewardItem() -- name: GetRewardItem
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	return v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("SPIN")
end
function v_u_1.Setup() -- name: Setup
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
	local v12 = v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("SETUP")
	for _, v13 in pairs(v12) do
		local v14 = v13[1]
		local v15 = v13[2]
		local v16 = v13[3]
		v_u_3:FindFirstChild(v16).Image.Image = v15
		v_u_3:FindFirstChild(v16).Value.Text = v14
	end
end
function v_u_1.Spin() -- name: Spin
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9, (ref) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6
	if v_u_9 then
		v_u_10.Visible = false
		v_u_9 = false
		local v17 = v_u_3.Rotation
		local v18 = v_u_1.GetRewardItem()
		if not v18 then
			v_u_10.Visible = true
			v_u_9 = true
			v_u_1.ShowError()
			return nil
		end
		local v19 = v17 + (v_u_11[v18[3]] - v17) % 360 + 7200
		local v20 = game:GetService("TweenService")
		local v21 = TweenInfo.new(9, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
		game.SoundService["Spinning Sound"]:Play()
		local v22 = v20:Create(v_u_3, v21, {
			["Rotation"] = v19
		})
		v22:Play()
		v22.Completed:Wait()
		if v18[4] == "WEAPONS" then
			game.SoundService["Mythical Summon"]:Play()
			local v23 = "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'>[Server Announcement]: " .. game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. " Spinned A </font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FF0000" .. "\'>" .. "Mythical" .. "</font>" .. "<font color=\'" .. "#FFFFFF" .. "\'> Weapon " .. v18[1] .. "</font>"
			if game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Announce") then
				game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Announce:FireServer(v23)
			end
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_8, v18[1], v18[2])
		else
			v_u_1.ShowReward(v_u_7, v18[1], v18[2])
		end
		v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("REWARD")
		v_u_9 = true
		v_u_10.Visible = true
	end
end
function v_u_1.ShowError() -- name: ShowError
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2
	local v_u_24 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("SpinError")
	local v_u_25 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Error")
	v_u_24.Visible = false
	(function() -- name: showWarning
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_25
		local v_u_26 = v_u_24:Clone()
		v_u_26.Parent = v_u_24.Parent
		v_u_26.Visible = true
		v_u_26.TextTransparency = 1
		v_u_26.Size = UDim2.fromScale(0.147, 0.065)
		v_u_26.Position = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
		v_u_25:Play()
		game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v_u_26, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
			["TextTransparency"] = 0,
			["Size"] = nil,
			["Position"] = nil,
			["Size"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.22, 0.065),
			["Position"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
		}):Play()
		task.delay(2.5, function()
			-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_26
			if v_u_26 then
				v_u_26:Destroy()
			end
		end)
	end)()
end
function v_u_1.ShowReward(p27, p28, p29) -- name: ShowReward
	p27.Image.Image = p29
	p27.RewardText.Text = p28
	p27.Visible = false
	local v30 = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local v31 = {
		["Size"] = p27.Size
	}
	p27.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	task.wait(0.1)
	p27.Visible = true
	v30:Create(p27, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), v31):Play()
	game.SoundService["VIP Weapon Reward"]:Play()
	task.wait(2)
	p27.Visible = false
end
function v_u_1.Start(p32) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_2 = p32
	v_u_3 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("Spinning Bar")
	v_u_4 = v_u_2.Spin
	v_u_5 = v_u_2.Amount
	v_u_7 = p32.Parent:FindFirstChild("NormalSpinReward")
	v_u_8 = p32.Parent:FindFirstChild("SpecialSpinReward")
	v_u_10 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild("Close")
	local v_u_33 = game.Workspace.Maps["Spinning Wheel"]:WaitForChild("Wheel"):WaitForChild("BillboardGui")["Free Spin Time"]
	local v_u_34 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	v_u_1.Setup()
	v_u_4.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1
		v_u_1.Spin()
	end)
	local v_u_35 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("Claim Free Spin")
	local function v_u_50() -- name: Timer
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_35, (copy) v_u_33
		if v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") == 0 then
			v_u_35.TextLabel.Text = "Claim Free Spin"
			v_u_33.Text = "Claim Free Spin"
		else
			local v36 = v_u_35.TextLabel
			local v37 = v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") or 0
			local v38 = v37 / 3600
			local v39 = math.floor(v38)
			local v40 = v37 % 3600 / 60
			local v41 = math.floor(v40)
			local v42 = v37 % 60
			v36.Text = string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d", v39, v41, v42) .. " For Free Spin"
			local v43 = v_u_33
			local v44 = v_u_34:GetAttribute("LastSpinReward") or 0
			local v45 = v44 / 3600
			local v46 = math.floor(v45)
			local v47 = v44 % 3600 / 60
			local v48 = math.floor(v47)
			local v49 = v44 % 60
			v43.Text = string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d", v46, v48, v49) .. " For Free Spin"
		end
	end
	v_u_50()
	v_u_34:GetAttributeChangedSignal("LastSpinReward"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_50
		v_u_50()
	end)
	v_u_35.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_6
		v_u_6.SpinWheel:InvokeServer("FREESPIN")
	end)
	v_u_34:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Spins"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_34, (ref) v_u_5
		if v_u_34:GetAttribute("Spins") then
			v_u_5.Text = "Spin: " .. v_u_34:GetAttribute("Spins")
		end
	end)
	if v_u_34:GetAttribute("Spins") then
		v_u_5.Text = "Spin: " .. v_u_34:GetAttribute("Spins")
	end
end
return v_u_1

-- [ModuleScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.InventoryHandlerOld

local _ = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui
local v_u_1 = nil
local v_u_2 = nil
local v_u_3 = nil

local v_u_5 = nil
local v_u_6 = nil

local function v_u_12(p10, p11) -- name: Unlock
	if p11 and p11 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p11 == "TITLES" then
			if p10:FindFirstChild("LockedButton") then
				p10.LockedButton.Visible = false
			end
			if p10:FindFirstChild("EquipButton") then
				p10.EquipButton.Visible = true
			end
		end
		return
	elseif p10 then
		p10.WeaponImage.Transparency = 0
		p10.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
		if p10.WeaponImage:FindFirstChild("Locked") then
			p10.WeaponImage.Locked.Visible = false
		end
		p10.EquipButton.Visible = true
		p10.LockedButton.Visible = false
	else
		print("Weapon Frame not Found")
	end
end
local function v_u_18(p13, _, p14) -- name: PrepareInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_6
	if p13 then
		if p14 and p14 == "TITLES" then
			print("nothing")
		else
			local v15 = v_u_7.Samples
			for _, v_u_16 in pairs(p13.Weapons) do
				local v17 = v_u_2.WeaponTemplate.TemplateLocked:Clone()
				v17.Name = v_u_16.weaponName
				v17.WeaponImage.Image.Image = v_u_16.image
				v17.WeaponImage.Image.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
				v17.WeaponName.Text = v_u_16.weaponName
				v17.WeaponName.TextColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.Rarity.Text = v_u_16.rarity
				v17.Rarity.TextColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.WeaponImage.Stroke.BackgroundColor3 = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Color
				v17.Parent = v_u_2
				v17.Visible = true
				v17.UIGradient.Color = v15[v_u_16.rarity].Gradient
				v17.EquipButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_16
					game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
					v_u_6.EquipWeapon:FireServer(v_u_16.weaponName)
				end)
			end
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
local function v_u_22() -- name: EquipWeapon
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_8, (ref) v_u_2
	local v19 = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("Equipped")
	if v19 then
		print("Last Weapon was " .. v19)
		if v_u_8 then
			v_u_8.TextLabel.Text = "Equip"
		end
		local v20 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild(v19)
		if v20 then
			print("Weapon Frame found for " .. v19)
			v20.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
			v_u_8 = v20.EquipButton
			print("Equipped Last Equipped")
		else
			print("Weapon Frame not found for " .. v19)
		end
	else
		print("No weapon equipped")
		local v21 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild("Baseball Bat")
		if v21 then
			print("Baseball Frame found")
			v21.EquipButton.TextLabel.Text = "Equipped"
			v_u_8 = v21.EquipButton
			return true
		end
		print("Baseball Frame not found")
		return
	end
end
function v_u_9.AddToInventory(p23, _, p24) -- name: AddToInventory
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_12, (ref) v_u_5
	if p24 and p24 ~= "WEAPONS" then
		if p24 == "TITLES" then
			print("TRYING TO FIND FRAME FOR " .. p23)
			local v25 = v_u_5:WaitForChild(p23, (1 / 0))
			if v25 then
				v_u_12(v25, p24)
			end
			print("FOUND AND UNLOCK " .. p23)
		end
		return
	end
	local v26 = nil
	local v27 = 0
	while not v26 do
		v27 = v27 + 1
		if v27 > 3 then
			break
		end
		v26 = v_u_2:FindFirstChild(p23)
		task.wait(1)
	end
	if v26 then
		print("Found Weapon Frame for " .. p23)
		v_u_12(v26, p24)
	else
		warn("Could not find frame for weapon:", p23)
	end
end
function v_u_9.Start(p28, p29) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_22
	v_u_1 = p28
	v_u_2 = v_u_1.Weapon.OutnerFrame.Weapons.InnerFrameLayout
	v_u_3 = p29
	v_u_4 = v_u_3.Titles
	v_u_5 = v_u_4.TitlesFrame
	v_u_6 = game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes
	v_u_7 = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponDatabase)
	v_u_8 = nil
	if v_u_1 then
		require(game.ReplicatedStorage.MainGuiHandler)
		v_u_1.Parent.Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1
			v_u_1.Visible = true
		end)
		v_u_1.CloseButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1
			v_u_1.Visible = false
		end)
		v_u_6.PrepareInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p30, p31, p32)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_9
			print(p32 .. " PREPARE INVENTORY")
			if p32 == "WEAPONS" then
				print("Weapons")
				v_u_18(p30, p31, "WEAPONS")
				for _, v33 in pairs(p31) do
					print("I have " .. v33)
				end
				for _, v34 in pairs(p31) do
					print("Doing for weapon " .. v34)
					v_u_9.AddToInventory(v34, p31, p32)
				end
			elseif p32 == "TITLES" then
				v_u_18(p30, p31, p32)
				for _, v35 in pairs(p31) do
					v_u_9.AddToInventory(v35, p31, "TITLES")
				end
			end
		end)
		v_u_6.AddToInventory.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p36, p37)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_9
			v_u_9.AddToInventory(p36, nil, p37)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_22
			while #v_u_2:GetChildren() < 10 do
				task.wait(1)
			end
			game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Equipped"):Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_22
				v_u_22()
			end)
			v_u_22()
		end)
	end
end
return v_u_9

					-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12
					v_u_12.Visible = false
				end)
			end)
		end

	v_u_20 = true
	v_u_19 = false

		v_u_15.Visible = false
	end

	end
end
function v_u_1.Fill() -- name: Fill
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_26, (ref) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_15

	for _, v_u_34 in ipairs(game.Workspace.Songs:GetChildren()) do

		v_u_35.Frame.NameLabel.Text = v_u_34.Name

			v_u_35.RedSelected.Visible = false
		end
		if v_u_35:FindFirstChild("BlueSelected") then
			v_u_35.BlueSelected.Visible = false
		end
		v_u_35.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_26, (copy) v_u_34, (copy) v_u_35, (ref) v_u_19, (ref) v_u_20, (ref) v_u_22, (ref) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_15
			if #v_u_26 > 0 then
				v_u_26[1]:Stop()
				v_u_26[2].Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
			end
			if v_u_34 then
				v_u_34.TimePosition = 0
				v_u_34:Play()
				v_u_26 = { v_u_34, v_u_35 }
			end
			v_u_35.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0, 1, 0)
			if v_u_19 then
				if v_u_20 then
					if v_u_22 == v_u_35 then
						print("This song is already selected for the Blue team!")
						return
					end
					if v_u_21 and v_u_21:FindFirstChild("RedSelected") then
						v_u_21.RedSelected.Visible = false
						v_u_21.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					end
					v_u_21 = v_u_35
					v_u_35.RedSelected.Visible = true
					v_u_20 = false
				else
					if v_u_21 == v_u_35 then
						print("This song is already selected for the Red team!")
						return
					end
					if v_u_22 and v_u_22:FindFirstChild("BlueSelected") then
						v_u_22.BlueSelected.Visible = false
						v_u_22.Frame.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
					end
					v_u_22 = v_u_35
					v_u_35.BlueSelected.Visible = true
					v_u_20 = true
				end
				if v_u_21 and (v_u_22 and v_u_15) then
					v_u_15.Visible = true
				end
			end
		end)
	end
end

============================================================
-- [ModuleScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.CashHandler
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v_u_1 = {}
local v_u_2 = nil
local v_u_3 = nil
local v_u_4 = nil
local v_u_5 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_6 = TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GameState")
function v_u_1.ThrowUI(p7) -- name: ThrowUI
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6
	local v8 = v_u_3
	v8.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("IsVip") and "+$50 For Winning" or "+$25 For Winning"
	if p7 then
		v8 = v_u_4
		v8.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("IsVip") and "+$60 For Killing Player" or "+$30 For Killing Player"
	end
	local v9 = v8:Clone()
	v9.Parent = v_u_2.Parent
	v9.Visible = true
	v_u_5:Create(v9, v_u_6, {
		["Position"] = nil,
		["TextTransparency"] = 1,
		["Position"] = UDim2.new(v9.Position.X.Scale, 0, v9.Position.Y.Scale - 0.4, 0)
	}):Play()
	local v_u_10 = game.SoundService["Cash Earned"]:Clone()
	v_u_10.Parent = game.SoundService.Temp
	v_u_10:Play()
	v_u_10.Ended:Once(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10
		v_u_10:Destroy()
	end)
end
function v_u_1.Start(p11) -- name: Start
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_1
	v_u_2 = p11
	v_u_3 = v_u_2.Parent:WaitForChild("GameWon")
	v_u_4 = v_u_2.Parent:WaitForChild("PlayerKilled")
	local v_u_12 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local v_u_13 = 0
	local v_u_14 = true
	local function v_u_21(p15) -- name: HandleCash
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_12, (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2, (ref) v_u_14
		if not v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash") then
			return
		end
		local v16 = v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash")
		if not p15 then
			local v17 = v_u_13 - v16
			if math.abs(v17) ~= 30 then
				local v18 = v_u_13 - v16
				if math.abs(v18) ~= 60 then
					local v19 = v_u_13 - v16
					if math.abs(v19) ~= 25 then
						local v20 = v_u_13 - v16
						if math.abs(v20) ~= 50 then
							goto l4
						end
					end
					v_u_1.ThrowUI(false)
					goto l4
				end
			end
			v_u_1.ThrowUI(true)
		end
		::l4::
		v_u_13 = v16
		v_u_2.Cash.Text = "$" .. v_u_12:GetAttribute("Cash")
		v_u_14 = false
	end
	v_u_12:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Cash"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_14
		v_u_21(v_u_14)
	end)
	v_u_21(v_u_14)
end
return v_u_1

	local v_u_10 = v_u_2.Options.Hitbox.Button
	local function v_u_13(p11) -- name: SFXVolumeChange
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_9
		for _, v12 in ipairs(game.SoundService:GetDescendants()) do
			if v12:IsA("Sound") and v12.Name ~= "Theme" then
				v12.Volume = p11 / 100
			end
		end
		v_u_9.Vol.Text = p11 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	end
	local v_u_14 = 50
	local v_u_15 = 50
	local v16 = v_u_15
	game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v16 / 100
	v_u_8.Vol.Text = v16 .. "%"
	game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()

		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_8
		local v17 = v_u_15 + 5
		v_u_15 = math.clamp(v17, 0, 100)
		local v18 = v_u_15
		game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v18 / 100
		v_u_8.Vol.Text = v18 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()

		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_8
		local v19 = v_u_15 - 5
		v_u_15 = math.clamp(v19, 0, 100)
		local v20 = v_u_15
		game.SoundService.Theme.Volume = v20 / 100
		v_u_8.Vol.Text = v20 .. "%"
		game.SoundService["UI Sound"].Hover:Play()
	end)
	v6.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_13
		local v21 = v_u_14 + 5
		v_u_14 = math.clamp(v21, 0, 100)
		v_u_13(v_u_14)
	end)
	v7.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_13
		local v22 = v_u_14 - 5
		v_u_14 = math.clamp(v22, 0, 100)
		v_u_13(v_u_14)
	end)

	for _, v24 in ipairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
		if v24.Character and v24.Character:WaitForChild("HitBox") then
			v24.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 1
		end

					p_u_25.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 0.999

		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_23

				end

				v_u_23 = true
				v_u_10.Text = "On"

				for _, v28 in ipairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
					v28.Character.HitBox.Transparency = 0.999
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end
