end)

local function v_u_48() -- name: clearList
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_18
	print("[LIST] Clearing player list")
	for _, v47 in pairs(v_u_16:GetChildren()) do
		if v47:IsA("Frame") and v47 ~= v_u_18 then
			v47:Destroy()

local function v_u_53(p_u_49) -- name: createPlayerEntry
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_28, (copy) v_u_32, (copy) v_u_9
	print("[LIST] Adding player:", p_u_49.Name)
	local v_u_50 = v_u_18:Clone()
	v_u_50.Visible = true
	v_u_50.Parent = v_u_16
	v_u_50.DisplayName.Text = p_u_49.DisplayName
	v_u_50.Username.Text = "@" .. p_u_49.Name
	task.spawn(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (copy) p_u_49, (copy) v_u_50
		local v51, v52 = pcall(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_3, (ref) p_u_49
			return v_u_3:GetUserThumbnailAsync(p_u_49.UserId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size100x100)
		end)
		if v51 then
			v_u_50.Profile.Image = v52
		end
	end)
	v_u_50.KickButton.Activated:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_49, (ref) v_u_28, (ref) v_u_32, (ref) v_u_9
		print("[CLIENT] Kick clicked on:", p_u_49.Name)
		if v_u_28 > 0 then
			v_u_32("Vote Kick is on cooldown")
		else
			v_u_9:FireServer(p_u_49)
		end
	end)
end
local function v_u_59(p54) -- name: refreshList
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_48, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_53
	print("[LIST] Refreshing list with filter:", p54)
	v_u_48()
	local v55 = string.lower(p54 or "")
	for _, v56 in ipairs(v_u_3:GetPlayers()) do
		if v56 ~= v_u_3.LocalPlayer then
			local v57 = string.lower(v56.Name)
			local v58 = string.lower(v56.DisplayName)
			if string.find(v57, v55) or string.find(v58, v55) then
				v_u_53(v56)
			end
		end
	end
end
task.defer(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_59
	print("[INIT] First refresh")
	v_u_59("")
	task.wait(0.5)
	print("[INIT] Second refresh")
	v_u_59("")
end)

script.Parent.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Cash.Value < 100 then
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Error Sound"]:Play()
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = true
		wait(2)
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = false
	else
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Buy Sound"]:Play()
		v_u_1:FireServer()
		script.Parent.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 1
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.Interactable = false
		wait(14)
		script.Parent.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 0
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.Interactable = true
	end
end)
script.Parent.Parent["Close Text"].MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	for _, v2 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v2.Name ~= "RewardSample" then
			v2.Visible = false
		end
	end
end)

	for _, v3 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v3.Name ~= "RewardSample" and (v3.Name ~= "SampleFrameBP" and (v3.Name ~= "ClickToClose" and (v3.Name ~= "Refund" and v3.Name ~= "Error1"))) then
			v3.Visible = true
		end
	end
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.FollowDeveloperReward.Frame.StatusLabel.Status
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: FireServer
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("ClaimFollowReward")
local v2 = script.Parent.Parent
local v_u_3 = v2:WaitForChild("ClaimButton")
local v_u_4 = v2:WaitForChild("StatusLabel")
local v_u_5 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Click")
local v_u_6 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Error")
v_u_3.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_4.Text = "\240\159\148\141 Checking follow status..."
	v_u_3.Active = false
	v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = false
	v_u_1:FireServer()
	task.delay(10, function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
		if v_u_4.Text == "\240\159\148\141 Checking follow status..." then
			v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 Request timed out. Try again."
			v_u_6:Play()
			v_u_3.Active = true
			v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = true
		end
	end)
end)
v_u_1.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p7, p8)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_3.Active = true
	v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = true
	if p7 == "SUCCESS" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\156\133 Reward claimed! +" .. p8 .. " Cash"
		v_u_5:Play()
		v_u_3.Text = "CLAIMED"
		v_u_3.Active = false
		return
	elseif p7 == "NOT_FOLLOWING" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\157\140 You must follow the developer to claim!"
		v_u_6:Play()
		return
	elseif p7 == "ALREADY_CLAIMED" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 You already claimed this reward."
		v_u_6:Play()
		v_u_3.Text = "CLAIMED"
		v_u_3.Active = false
	else
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 Something went wrong. Try again later."
		v_u_6:Play()
	end
end)

local function v5(p2, p3) -- name: createText
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	local v4 = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	v4.Size = UDim2.new(1, -15, 0, 0)
	v4.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	v4.TextWrapped = true
	v4.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	v4.Font = Enum.Font.FredokaOne
	v4.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	v4.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
	v4.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	v4.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
	if p3 == "Date" then
		v4.TextSize = 26
		v4.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	elseif p3 == "Title" then
		v4.TextSize = 23
		v4.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	elseif p3 == "Content" then
		v4.TextSize = 15
		v4.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	end
	v4.Text = p2
	v4.Parent = v_u_1
	return v4
end

		["Content"] = { " Added 40+ New Songs", " Added New Quests System" }
	}
}) do
	v5("\240\159\147\133 Update " .. v6.Date, "Date")
	v5(v6.Title, "Title")
	for _, v7 in ipairs(v6.Content) do
		v5("\226\128\162 " .. v7, "Content")
	end
	local v8 = Instance.new("Frame")
	v8.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 15)
	v8.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	v8.Parent = v_u_1
end
local v_u_9 = v_u_1:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIListLayout")
if v_u_9 then
	v_u_9:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_9
		v_u_1.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, v_u_9.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 10)
	end)
end

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.Mythical Crate.MythicalFrame.FastSpin.LocalScript
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: FireServer
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game.ReplicatedStorage.SpinEvent
script.Parent.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Cash.Value < 100 then
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Error Sound"]:Play()
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = true
		wait(2)
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = false
	else
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Buy Sound"]:Play()
		v_u_1:FireServer()
		script.Parent.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 1
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.Interactable = false
		wait(14)
		script.Parent.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 0
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.Interactable = true
	end
end)
script.Parent.Parent["Close Text"].MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	for _, v2 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v2.Name ~= "RewardSample" then
			v2.Visible = false
		end
	end
end)
game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.SpinFrameOpen.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
	for _, v3 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v3.Name ~= "RewardSample" and (v3.Name ~= "SampleFrameBP" and (v3.Name ~= "ClickToClose" and (v3.Name ~= "Refund" and v3.Name ~= "Error1"))) then
			v3.Visible = true
		end
	end
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.Mythical Crate.MythicalFrame.FastSpin.LocalScript [2]
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: ProximityPrompt, Marketplace
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")
local v_u_2 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
script.Parent.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_2
	local v3, v4 = pcall(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2
		return v_u_1:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(v_u_2.UserId, 1663157605)
	end)
	if not (v3 and v4) then
		v_u_1:PromptGamePassPurchase(v_u_2, 1663157605)
	end
end)

})

end)

-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.Setting.Frame.Server Time.Server Time
-- Method: decompile()
============================================================
local v1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("ServerTimeEvent")
local v_u_2 = script.Parent
v1.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p3)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2
	local v4 = v_u_2
	local v5 = p3 / 3600
	local v6 = math.floor(v5)
	local v7 = p3 % 3600 / 60
	local v8 = math.floor(v7)
	local v9 = p3 % 60
	v4.Text = string.format("Server Time: %02dh %02dm %02ds", v6, v8, v9)
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.FollowDeveloperReward.Frame.StatusLabel.Status
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: FireServer
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("ClaimFollowReward")
local v2 = script.Parent.Parent
local v_u_3 = v2:WaitForChild("ClaimButton")
local v_u_4 = v2:WaitForChild("StatusLabel")
local v_u_5 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Click")
local v_u_6 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Error")
v_u_3.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_4.Text = "\240\159\148\141 Checking follow status..."
	v_u_3.Active = false
	v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = false
	v_u_1:FireServer()
	task.delay(10, function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_6, (ref) v_u_3
		if v_u_4.Text == "\240\159\148\141 Checking follow status..." then
			v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 Request timed out. Try again."
			v_u_6:Play()
			v_u_3.Active = true
			v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = true
		end
	end)
end)
v_u_1.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p7, p8)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_3.Active = true
	v_u_3.AutoButtonColor = true
	if p7 == "SUCCESS" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\156\133 Reward claimed! +" .. p8 .. " Cash"
		v_u_5:Play()
		v_u_3.Text = "CLAIMED"
		v_u_3.Active = false
		return
	elseif p7 == "NOT_FOLLOWING" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\157\140 You must follow the developer to claim!"
		v_u_6:Play()
		return
	elseif p7 == "ALREADY_CLAIMED" then
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 You already claimed this reward."
		v_u_6:Play()
		v_u_3.Text = "CLAIMED"
		v_u_3.Active = false
	else
		v_u_4.Text = "\226\154\160\239\184\143 Something went wrong. Try again later."
		v_u_6:Play()
	end
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.Mythical Crate.MythicalFrame.FastSpin.LocalScript
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: FireServer
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game.ReplicatedStorage.SpinEvent
script.Parent.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Cash.Value < 100 then
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Error Sound"]:Play()
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = true
		wait(2)
		script.Parent.Parent.Error1.Visible = false
	else
		game:GetService("SoundService")["Buy Sound"]:Play()
		v_u_1:FireServer()
		script.Parent.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 1
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 1
		script.Parent.Interactable = false
		wait(14)
		script.Parent.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 0
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.Interactable = true
	end
end)
script.Parent.Parent["Close Text"].MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	for _, v2 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v2.Name ~= "RewardSample" then
			v2.Visible = false
		end
	end
end)
game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.SpinFrameOpen.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
	for _, v3 in ipairs(script.Parent.Parent:GetChildren()) do
		if v3.Name ~= "RewardSample" and (v3.Name ~= "SampleFrameBP" and (v3.Name ~= "ClickToClose" and (v3.Name ~= "Refund" and v3.Name ~= "Error1"))) then
			v3.Visible = true
		end
	end
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.StarterGui.Mythical Crate.MythicalFrame.FastSpin.LocalScript [2]
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: ProximityPrompt, Marketplace
============================================================
local v_u_1 = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")
local v_u_2 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
script.Parent.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_2
	local v3, v4 = pcall(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_2
		return v_u_1:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(v_u_2.UserId, 1663157605)
	end)
	if not (v3 and v4) then
		v_u_1:PromptGamePassPurchase(v_u_2, 1663157605)
	end
end)

		script.Parent.TextTransparency = 0
		script.Parent.UIStroke.Transparency = 0
		script.Parent.Interactable = true
	end
end)

-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v1 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_2 = script.Parent.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("Revives Store")
local v3 = v_u_2:WaitForChild("UIScale")
local v_u_4 = game:GetService("SoundService"):WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Click")
local v5 = script.Parent
local v_u_6 = v1:Create(v3, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
	["Scale"] = 1
})
v_u_2.Visible = false
v3.Scale = 0.8
v5.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_2.Visible = true
	v_u_4:Play()
	v_u_6:Play()
end)

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_2
	v_u_4:Play()
	v_u_2.Visible = false

	["mproll7117_2"] = true

	v1.Visible = true

	v1.Visible = false
end

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.Emote.Shop.ScrollingFrame.OutnerFrame.InnerFrameLayout.Button
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: FireServer, Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v1 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local v2 = game:GetService("Players")
local v_u_3 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v4 = v2.LocalPlayer
local v_u_5 = v1:WaitForChild("RemoteEvents")
local v_u_6 = v4.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("Emote"):WaitForChild("Shop")
local v_u_7 = {}
local v_u_8 = v_u_6:WaitForChild("WarningText")
local v_u_9 = game.SoundService:WaitForChild("UI Sound"):WaitForChild("Error")
v_u_8.Visible = false
local function v_u_11() -- name: showWarning
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_3
	local v_u_10 = v_u_8:Clone()
	v_u_10.Parent = v_u_8.Parent
	v_u_10.Visible = true
	v_u_10.TextTransparency = 1
	v_u_10.Size = UDim2.fromScale(0.147, 0.065)
	v_u_10.Position = UDim2.fromScale(0.42, 0.49)
	v_u_9:Play()
	v_u_3:Create(v_u_10, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		["TextTransparency"] = 0,
		["Size"] = nil,
		["Position"] = nil,
		["Size"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.22, 0.065),
		["Position"] = UDim2.fromScale(0.384, 0.488)
	}):Play()
	task.delay(2.5, function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10
		if v_u_10 then
			v_u_10:Destroy()
		end
	end)
end
local function v_u_18(p12, p13) -- name: updateEmoteFrame
	local v14 = p12:GetAttribute("EmoteName")
	p12:GetAttribute("Price")
	if v14 and p13 then
		local v15 = p12:FindFirstChild("BuyButton", true)
		if v15 then
			if p13.Owned[v14] then
				local v16 = p13.Equipped
				local v17 = v16[1] == v14 and 1 or (v16[2] == v14 and 2 or (v16[3] == v14 and 3 or (v16[4] == v14 and 4 or nil)))
				if v17 then
					v15.TextLabel.Text = "Unequip (Slot " .. v17 .. ")"
				else
					v15.TextLabel.Text = "Equip"
				end
			else
				v15.TextLabel.Text = "Buy"
				return
			end
		else
			return
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
local function v_u_20() -- name: updateAll
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_18, (ref) v_u_7
	for _, v19 in ipairs(v_u_6:GetDescendants()) do
		if v19:IsA("Frame") and v19:GetAttribute("EmoteName") then
			v_u_18(v19, v_u_7)
		end
	end
end
v_u_5.UpdateEmoteData.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p21)
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_20
	v_u_7 = p21
	v_u_20()
end)
v_u_5.BuyFailed.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11
	v_u_11()
end)
local v_u_22 = v_u_7
for _, v23 in ipairs(v_u_6:GetDescendants()) do
	if v23:IsA("Frame") and v23:GetAttribute("EmoteName") then
		local v_u_24 = v23:GetAttribute("EmoteName")
		local v_u_25 = v23:GetAttribute("Price")
		local v26 = v23:FindFirstChild("BuyButton", true)
		if v26 then
			v26.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_25
				if v_u_22 and v_u_22.Owned then
					if v_u_22.Owned[v_u_24] then
						v_u_5.EquipEmote:FireServer(v_u_24)
					else
						v_u_5.BuyEmote:FireServer(v_u_24, v_u_25)
					end
				else
					return
				end
			end)
		end
	end
end
task.wait(0.2)
v_u_5.RequestEmoteData:FireServer()

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.Not Used UI.VoteKickUI.VoteResult.Passed.CloseButton.Close (Quests)
-- Method: decompile()
============================================================

local v_u_4 = v3.Hover:Clone()
local v5 = v3.Click:Clone()
v_u_4.Parent = v1
v5.Parent = v1
v1.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_2
	v_u_4:Play()
	v_u_2.Visible = false
end)

============================================================
-- [LocalScript]  Path: game.Players.usnsbsbsb3.PlayerGui.Inventory.Frame.Background.WeaponFrame.Buttons.ScrollingFrame.AllButton.Tween
-- Method: decompile()
-- Tags: Tween
-- EXTERNAL:
--   >> TweenService used (animation/timing)
============================================================
local v_u_1 = script.Parent
local v_u_2 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_3 = v_u_1.Size
local v_u_4 = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut)
local function v_u_6(p5) -- name: makeTween
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_4
	return v_u_2:Create(v_u_1, v_u_4, {
		["Size"] = UDim2.new(v_u_3.X.Scale * p5, v_u_3.X.Offset * p5, v_u_3.Y.Scale * p5, v_u_3.Y.Offset * p5)
	})
end
v_u_1.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_6(1.1):Play()
end)
v_u_1.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_6(1):Play()
end)
v_u_1.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	local v7 = v_u_6(0.9)
	local v_u_8 = v_u_6(1)
	v7:Play()
	v7.Completed:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
		v_u_8:Play()
	end)
end)

		["Size"] = UDim2.new(v_u_3.X.Scale * p5, v_u_3.X.Offset * p5, v_u_3.Y.Scale * p5, v_u_3.Y.Offset * p5)
	})
end
v_u_1.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_6(1.1):Play()
end)
v_u_1.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	v_u_6(1):Play()
end)
v_u_1.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	local v7 = v_u_6(0.9)
	local v_u_8 = v_u_6(1)
	v7:Play()
	v7.Completed:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
		v_u_8:Play()
	end)
end)
